ActionBarLayout_android_layout_gravity
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

.. java:field:: public static final int ActionBarLayout_android_layout_gravity
   :outertype: R.styleable

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`android.R.attr.layout_gravity`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`ActionBarLayout`\  array.

   Must be one or more (separated by '|') of the following constant values.

   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | Constant          | Value  | Description |
   +===================+========+=============+
   | bottom            | 50     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | center            | 11     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | center_horizontal | 1      |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | center_vertical   | 10     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | clip_horizontal   | 8      |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | clip_vertical     | 80     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | end               | 800005 |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | fill              | 77     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | fill_horizontal   | 7      |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | fill_vertical     | 70     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | left              | 3      |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | right             | 5      |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | start             | 800003 |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+
   | top               | 30     |             |
   +-------------------+--------+-------------+

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

.. java:field:: public static final int ActionBar_backgroundSplit
   :outertype: R.styleable

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`ru.sibur.android.garbagecollector.dev.R.attr.backgroundSplit`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`ActionBar`\  array.

ActionBar_contentInsetEnd
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

.. java:field:: public static final int ActionBar_contentInsetEnd
   :outertype: R.styleable

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`ru.sibur.android.garbagecollector.dev.R.attr.contentInsetEnd`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`ActionBar`\  array.

   May be a dimension value, which is a floating point number appended with a unit such as "\ ``14.5sp``\ ". Available units are: px (pixels), dp (density-independent pixels), sp (scaled pixels based on preferred font size), in (inches), and mm (millimeters).

AppCompatTextView_autoSizeStepGranularity
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

.. java:field:: public static final int AppCompatTextView_autoSizeStepGranularity
   :outertype: R.styleable

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`ru.sibur.android.garbagecollector.dev.R.attr.autoSizeStepGranularity`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`AppCompatTextView`\  array.

   May be a dimension value, which is a floating point number appended with a unit such as "\ ``14.5sp``\ ". Available units are: px (pixels), dp (density-independent pixels), sp (scaled pixels based on preferred font size), in (inches), and mm (millimeters).

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`ru.sibur.android.garbagecollector.dev.R.attr.actionBarSize`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`AppCompatTheme`\  array.

   May be a dimension value, which is a floating point number appended with a unit such as "\ ``14.5sp``\ ". Available units are: px (pixels), dp (density-independent pixels), sp (scaled pixels based on preferred font size), in (inches), and mm (millimeters).

   Must be one of the following constant values.

   +--------------+-------+-------------+
   | Constant     | Value | Description |
   +==============+=======+=============+
   | wrap_content | 0     |             |
   +--------------+-------+-------------+

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`ru.sibur.android.garbagecollector.dev.R.attr.layout_constraintWidth_max`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`ConstraintLayout_Layout`\  array.

   May be a dimension value, which is a floating point number appended with a unit such as "\ ``14.5sp``\ ". Available units are: px (pixels), dp (density-independent pixels), sp (scaled pixels based on preferred font size), in (inches), and mm (millimeters).

SearchView_android_maxWidth
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

.. java:field:: public static final int SearchView_android_maxWidth
   :outertype: R.styleable

   This symbol is the offset where the \ :java:ref:`android.R.attr.maxWidth`\  attribute's value can be found in the \ :java:ref:`SearchView`\  array.

   May be a dimension value, which is a floating point number appended with a unit such as "\ ``14.5sp``\ ". Available units are: px (pixels), dp (density-independent pixels), sp (scaled pixels based on preferred font size), in (inches), and mm (millimeters).
